10a5(1): thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra sA d+hu// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid phye/ 
10a6(1): bya bar gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje dgyes pa'i ngang
10a7(1): su gnas so// de nas rdo rje dgyes pa'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshes
10a8(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi legs so zhes bya ba la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams byas nas rdo rje
10b1(1): 'dzin ni shin tu dga' bar byed pa dang / rab tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dzes par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' rab tu dga' ba'i

10b3(1): legs byin nang na bdag mchog pas// rnam rtog bral ba de dag gi/ nges par dgyes pa bskyed yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rab tu
10b4(1): de bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs kha nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyab na/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bka' nid
10b5(1): gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa
10b6(1): thams cad kyi rab tu dgyes pa bla na med pa'i ye shes kyi dam tshig sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i sems can thams cad mgu bar bya ba dang / thams cad
10b7(1): bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgyes pa'i ro bla na med pa dam pa 'grub pa thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir rdo rje dgyes
10b8(1): pa de byang chub sems dpa' chen po rab tu dga' ba'i rgyal po de'i lag tu de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje dgyes pa zhes rdo rje zhes bya
11a1(1): ba'i dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje dgyes pas/ rdo rje dgyes pa'i dbyibs des de
11a2(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la legs so zhes bya bas rab tu dgyes par byed cing ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi legs byin pa/ 'di ni
11a3(1): rab tu 'jug byed pas// rdo rje thams cad dgyes par byed lta rdzas dgyes baspel ba'o// // byang chub sems dpa' chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
11a4(1): spyan drang ba'i dam tshig dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i ye shes dang / dgyes pa chen po dang / 'di bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig
11a5(1): chen na po'i sems dpa'o// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i dam tshig las byung ba rin po che'i byin gyi brgya byas rdo rje nyes
11a6(1): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin ga
11a7(1): po rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra rat+na/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni rdo rje sems pa
11a8(1): nam mkha' dang mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes shin tu rtogs pa yin pa'i phyir ro// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de nam mkha' thams

11b3(1): dpa'i ting nge 'dzin shin tu bsgoms par gyur pa'i phyir/ yang nam mkha'i khams thams cad las byung ba 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mnyan
11b4(1): rje rin po che chen po'i dbyibs su gyur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje rin po che'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams
11b5(1): shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi skur gyur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang la sogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
11b6(1): rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi snying po las shin tu byung ba dang / 
11b7(1): rab tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas/ 
11b8(1): nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di cheng du brjod do// e ma'o chags med rgyal ba yang // khams gsum dbang por dgongs pas na// rdo rje rin chen dam pa yi// dbang gi mchog ni
12a1(1): bdag yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i lus de bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa
12a2(1): thams cad kyi spyan sngun/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams na
12a3(1): kyi nor bu rin po che rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhi gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i dam tshig dang / 
12a4(1): sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i don thams cad yongs su grub par bya ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshes
12a5(1): pa thams cad kyi don phur sum tshigs pa'i grub pa thob par bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i rdo rje rin po che chen po 'khor lo bya
12a6(1): rje rin po che myu gu'i dbang gis dbang bskur nas/ lag tu rdo rje'i nor bu de byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje snying
12a7(1): ba'i dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying pos rdo rje'i nor bu de rang gi dbang bskur ba'i gnas su 'a
12a8(1): che du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi sems dpa'i dbyings// dbang bskur de ni bdag yin te// bdag gi lag tu byin pas na// rin chen len
12b1(1): yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzi brjid chen po zhes bya ba'i dam tshig las byung ba'i rin po che'i byin gyi brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba
12b2(1): par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra ti dza/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams
12b3(1): thag pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de nyi ma'i dkyil khor chen por gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs
12b4(1): nas/ rdo rje nyi ma'i dbyibs su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'ad ste phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje nyi ma'i dkyil khor 'khor de las 'jig rten gyi khams tha
12b5(1): tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer 'gyed pa la sogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
12b6(1): rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems ngo ba'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu gzi brjid che ba nyid dang / shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur te/ byang chub sems
12b7(1): dpa' chen po gzi brjid chen po'i skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ ched du brjod pa 'di cheng du brjod do// e ma'o sems can
12b8(1): khams kun du/ snang byed gzi brjid dpe med bdag/ gang phyir sangs rgyas dag pa yi// 'dren pa rnams kyang sbyong bar byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po dri ma med pa'i
13a1(1): gzi brjid de'i lus bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi g.yas phyogs su zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas te
13a2(1): bka' rod cing bcugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor gyi byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la sdom
13a3(1): poro zhugasu nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer gyi dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams kyi gzi brjid mtshungs pa med pa
13a4(1): dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi 'od 'thob cing dngos grub dam pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi
13a5(1): phyir/ rdo rje nyi ma de byang chub dpa' chen po gzi brjid chen po de'i lag du de bzhin du byin no// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje'i 'od ces rdo rje zhes bya ba'i
13a6(1): dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje 'od rdo rje nyi ma nges de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la snang bar byed cing / ched du brjod po
13a7(1): spangs rgyas kun gyi snang ba 'di// mi shes mun nag 'joms byed pa// shin tu phra rdul ji snyed pa'i// nyi ma'i 'od pas shin tu lhag/ de nas yang bcom ldan la/ 
13a8(1): sems dpa' chen po rin chen dpal gyi dam tshig las byung ba rin po che'i byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin ga
13b1(1): cad kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i dam tshig zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra ke du/ den
13b2(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni/ bcon ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid de/ rgyal mtshan kha dog dang gzugs dang rgyan dang dbyibs san
13b3(1): byang nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dbyibs su gyur te/ phyag gnyis su
13b4(1): rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin ga
13b5(1): cad kyi rin po che'i rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rin po che chen po'i dpal/ 
13b6(1): dang shin tu brtan pa yin pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po rin po che dbal gyi skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnamasar snang mdzad kyi
13b7(1): thugs la gnas nas/ ched du brjod pa 'ang ched du brjod do// e ma'o// don kun grub pa dang / dgongs pa thams cad rdzogs pa yi// don rnams thams cad rdzogs byed pa'i// 
13b8(1): 'dra med dpal ni bdag yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rin po che'i dpal gyi sku bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs kha nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
14a1(1): g.yon gyi phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa
14a2(1): thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan gyi byin gyi rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nor bu yid bzhin gyi rgyal mtshan bsgrang
14a3(1): ba'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams kyi re ba thams cad yongs su bskang bar bya ba dang thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar
14a4(1): bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi don chen po'i dngos grub dam pa thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan de byang chub sems dpa' chen
14a5(1): bo rin po che'i dpal de'i lag du de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba ni rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro// 
14a6(1): nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sgo
14a7(1): ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi dgongs pa kun// yongs su rdzogs par byed pa yi// yid bzhin nor bu rgyal mtshan 'di// sbyin pa
14a8(1): pa'i tshul// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po'i dam tshig las byung ba rin po che'i
14b1(1): brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi dgyes pa'i dam tshig zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa
14b2(1): kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra hAs/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa 'di ni/ bcom ldan 'ang/ 
14b3(1): ba nyid de de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dzum par gyur te/ byung nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres
14b4(1): rdo rje 'dzum pa'i dbyibs su gyur te phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje 'dzum pa'i dbyibs de las/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin phra ba dang
14b5(1): ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chang du byung ba la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul
14b6(1): rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i tong nge 'dzin ni rtag tu dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po yin pa dang shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang
14b7(1): chub sems dpa' chen po rtag tu dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po'i lus su gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ ched du brjod

15a5(1): cad kyi dbang po yongs su spong ba'i ye shes mngon par shes pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang
15a6(1): bo de'i lag tu rdo rje 'dzum pa de de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje dga' ba rdo rje dga' zhes rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro// 
15a7(1): nas byang chen sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje dga' bas/ rdo rje 'dzum pa des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgyes par byed cing / ched du brjo
15a8(1): du brjod do// 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rmang du 'byung bskyed ston pa po// dgyes chen byed pa'i ye shes te/ gtsug lag gzhan gyis shes
15b1(1): dbang bskur ba ni chen po dang / 'od kyi dkyil khor 'dom gang ba dang / sems dpa' chen po'i don dang / dgyes pa chen po dang / 'di bzhi ni de bzhin gsheg
15b2(1): cad kyi dbang bskur ba chen po'i sems dpa'o// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun du spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang ba
15b3(1): las byung ba'i chos kyi byin gyi brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dam tshig zhes bya

15b5(1): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rang bzhin gyis dag pa'i chos mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rab du rtogs pa'i phyir/ dam pa'i
15b6(1): chos kyi 'od zer du gyur de byung ngo // dam pa'i chos kyi 'od zer de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du kun tu snang bar byas nas chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin du gyur to// 
15b7(1): chos kyi dbyings de dag thams cad kyang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad dang mnyam par
15b8(1): 'jug pa'i tshad tsam gyi rdo rje pad+ma chen po'i dbyings su gyur te/ phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje pad+ma'i dbyings de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul phra mo dang mnyam

16a2(1): rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po yin

16a5(1): 'dra'i chos rnams las// rnam par dag pa dmigs par gyur/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi lus de bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi

16a7(1): pa thams cad kyi zhing nge 'dzin gyi mnyam pa zhing ye shes dam tshig las byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rnam par spang na
16a8(1): dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams kyi bdag dang gzhan rnam par dag par bya ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar
16b1(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi ye shes dang mngon par shes pa drug thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras
16b2(1): kyi dbang po dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba nyid dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos sku'i dbang gis dbang bskur nas/ de'i lag tu byin no// de bzhin gyis
16b3(1): pa thams cad kyis rdo rje'i spyan rdo rje'i zhes rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang skur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje spyan gyis rdo rje'i pad+mo'i 'dab mdze
16b4(1): 'byed pas/ 'dod chags rnam par dag cing ma chags pa'i ngo bo nyid du gzigs pas gzigs shing ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi 'dod chags kyi/ 
16b5(1): de yi kho na rtogs pa 'di// bdag sde bdag gi lag du byin// chos la chos ni gnas par gyur// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal
16b6(1): gyi dam tshig las byung ba'i chos kyi byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab dang ye shes chen po'i
16b7(1): dam tshig ces bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra tik+ta/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma thag pa
16b8(1): 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid de shes rab kyi ye shes kyi ral gring gyur te/ byang nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par
17a1(1): gyur nas/ rdo rje ral gri'i dbyibs su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje ral gri'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi
17a2(1): khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab kyi ye shes la sogs pa dang / 
17a3(1): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams bya ste/ rdo rje sems dpo'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu 'jam pa'i dpal yin pa dang / shin tu brtan pa yin pa'i phyir
17a4(1): gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i skur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas nas
17a5(1): ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// 'jam dbyangs bdag ni yin par dgongs// gang phyir shes rab gzugs med kyang / 
17a6(1): dbyangs nyid du ni dmigs pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gyi sku de bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams
17a7(1): cad kyi g.yas phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa tham/ 
17a8(1): cad kyi shes rab kyi ye shes kyi rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa thams cad gtsang / 
17b1(1): tshig dang / sems cad kyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i sdug bsngal thams cad bcad ba dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas
17b2(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi rjes su 'brang ba'i shes rab dam pa yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ rdo rje ral gri de byang chub sem/ 
17b3(1): dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gyi lag tu de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i blo rdo rje'i blo zhes bya ba'i rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur
17b4(1): de nas chu byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i blos de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rdo rje'i ral gri nges 'debs shing / ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// 
17b5(1): 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i tshul// dgra rnams thams cad gcod byed cing / sdig pa thams cad 'joms pa'i mchog/ 
17b6(1): de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i dam tshig las byung ba chos kyi byin brlabs
17b7(1): rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs po thams cad kyi 'khor lo'i dam tshig ces bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
17b8(1): snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra he du/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung zag pa 'di ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa
18a1(1): de nyid rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po la sogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor du gyur te byung nas/ bcom ldan 'ang
18a2(1): rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje 'khor lo'i dbyibs su gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi phyag gnyis su gnas par gyur to// 
18a3(1): de nas rdo rje 'khor lo'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku rnams byung ste/ sems bskyed
18a4(1): ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul dang chos 'phrul rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byas te/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting
18a5(1): nge 'dzin ni sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yin pa dang / shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po sems
18a6(1): bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba zhes bya ba'i skur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas nas/ cheng du brjod pa 'di che du brjod do// 
18a7(1): rdo rje dam pa chos can gyi// e ma'o rdo rje 'khor lo bdag/ gang phyir sems bskyed tsam gyis kyang // chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gyur// de nas byang chub sems dpa/ 
18a8(1): chen po sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i sku de/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi g.yon phyogs
18b1(1): dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo rdo rje zhes bya
18b2(1): nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor chen po'i dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med par 'ju
18b3(1): phyi mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang // thams cad kyi bde ba dang yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dam pa 'grub
18b4(1): pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir/ rdo rje'i 'khor lo de byang chub sems dpa' chen po sems bskyed ma thag pa chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de'i lag tu de bzhin gshegs pa
18b5(1): thams cad kyis rdo rje snying po zhes rdo rje snying po zhes rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying pos rdo rje'i 'khor
18b6(1): lo nges de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad phyir mi ldog pa nyid du 'jog cing / ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// chos rnams thams
18b7(1): cad rnam par spyod// phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo ni// byang chub snying po yin par bshad// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po mi gsung ba'i
18b8(1): dam tshig las byung ba/ chos kyi byin gyis brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bzlas pa'i dam tshig
19a1(1): ces bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra b+hA Sha/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las
19a2(1): byung ma thag pa 'di bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de nyid de/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos nyid kyi yi ger gyur te byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad
19a3(1): kyi thugasu zhugs te gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje bzlas pa'i dbyibasu gyur te phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje'i bzlas pa'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi kham
19a4(1): thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang / mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos nyid la sogs pa dang / sangs
19a5(1): rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang la sogs pa byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu tshig ma yin pa dang / shin tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur
19a6(1): tri/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po tshig ma yin pa'i skur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// 
19a7(1): e ma'o rang 'byung rnams kyi gsang // ldem po ngag du bdag dgongs te// gang phyir dam pa'i chos 'chang ba// tshig tu spos las rnam par bral// de nas byang chub sems/ 
19a8(1): dpa' tshig ma yin pa'i spang // bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyab na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ yang bkra
19b1(1): nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i gsung rdo rje'i dam tshig las byung ba zhes bya ba'i
19b2(1): ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi ye shes kyi dam tshig dang / sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa
19b3(1): med pa rnams kyi tshig grub dang / thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi gsang ba nyid thob pa'i
19b4(1): dngos grub dam pa'i bar gyi phyir// rdo rje bzlas pa de byang chub sems dpa' chen po tshig ma yin pa'i lag tu de bzhin du byin no// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
19b5(1): kyis rdo rje'i tshig rdo rje'i tshig zhes rdo rje ming gi dbang gis dbang bskur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i tshig gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rdo
19b6(1): rje'i bzlas pa des yang dag par smra zhing ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rdo rje bzlas par brjod pa yin// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
19b7(1): cad kyi// sngags 'di myur du 'grub par gyur// rdo rje chos nyid kyi ye shes dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab kyi ye shes dang / chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bskor ba'i
19b8(1): ye shes dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi spros pa rnam par ldog pa'i ye shes te/ 'di bzhi ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi sems dpa' chen po'o// 
20a1(1): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub sems dpa' chen po las thams cad pa zhes bya ba'i dam tshig las byung ba
20a2(1): las kyi byin brlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dam tshig ces bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs
20a3(1): pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kha nas phyung ngo // badz+ra kar+m+ma/ de nas rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni las thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes shin tu rtogs

20a5(1): kyi 'od gzer du gyur te byung nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi 'od gzer de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar bya nas/ de bzhin
20a6(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dbyings lta bur gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dbyings ma lus pa de yang bcom ldan 'angs rnam par
20a7(1): snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs te/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad dang mnyam pa'i tshad tsam du gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las kyi dbyings de
20a8(1): las/ las kyi rdo rje'i dbyibs su gyur nas phyag gnyis su gnas so// de nas rdo rje'i dbyibs de las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i/ 
20b1(1): de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku rnams byung ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'grin las la sogs pa dang / sangs rgyas thams
20b2(1): cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul rnams byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las mtha' yas pa yin pa dang / shin tu brtan
20b3(1): pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las thams cad ces bya ba'i skur gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das
20b4(1): rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs khar gnas nas/ cheng du brjod du pa 'di ched du brjod do// e malo sangs rgyas rnams kyi nges// 'phrin las mang po kun bdag yin// sangs rgyas
20b5(1): don ni lhun grub phyir// rdo rje las ni 'jug par gyur/ de byang chub sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las thams cad ces bya ba'i lus bcom ldan
20b6(1): 'das kyi thugs las byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyan sngar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas te yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur
20b7(1): to/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdon mi za ba'i dam tshig las byung ba rdo rje'i byin gyis brlabs zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhug
20b8(1): nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mched bar bya ba la sogs pa gdon mi za ba tshad med pa dang / las kyi cho ga rgyas pa thams cad kyi dam tshig dang sems can gyi khas
33a1(1): babang ba/ phyag 'tshal rdo rje drag po la// brdzun na/ rdo rje chams sbyor rab bsdus ny-id// rdo rje 'dzing bar bkrol byed// dri khwa chung ngam tshig mchog/ brag 'a
33a2(1): rdo rje khu chung la// su zhig mi snang bla ni// ni brgya dang rtsa brgyang 'di// rdo rje mi dbang bskur lo sogs// mchog rnams kun gyi de dbang bskur// gang zhig yon tan ming rnams kyis// rdo rje
33a3(1): 'chang ba chen po la// rtag tu dbyangs kyis bstod na ni// de yang rdo rje 'chang 'drar 'gyur// ming brgya rtsa brgyad 'di dag gis// bdag cag gi ni bstong pa yin// theg pa chen po rtogs pa
33a4(1): yin// tshul chen yang ni rgyas par mdzod// mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// sangs rgyas kun gyi 'khor chen+d+ra blo dam pa yi// cho ga mchog ni bshad par gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das
33a5(1): rdo rje chen po 'dzin pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba'i tshig 'di thos nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig 'byung ba'i rdo rje'i byin gyis brlabs pa zhes
33a6(1): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// rdo rje dbyings zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di bshad do// // de nas yang dag bshang bgyi ba// dkyil 'khor chen po dam pa ste// rdo rje
33a7(1): dbyings dang 'dra bas na// rdo rje dbyings zhes bya bar grags// sems dpa' chen po'i phyag rgya cher// bsgom zhing byin gyis brlabs bgyid cing // dkyil 'khor gyi ni dbus nyid du/ 
33a8(1): ci rigs par ni mchis nas kyang // phyag rgya la gnas bzhin langs// kun tu rnam par bltas nas ni// rdo rje sems dpa' zhes brjod nas// bsgyings pa'i tshul gyis yongs su bskor// 
33b1(1): sang ba legs par bkal nas kyang // chad dang mthun par mdzes pa yi// thig gis mkhas pas tsa nus kyis// dkyil 'khor gyi ni thig gdab cing // gru bzhir bgyi zhing sgo bzhi dang // na
33b2(1): babs bzhis ni mdzes la// thig bzhi dang ni ldan 'gyur ba// ngar dang me tog baphreng bas brgyan// grwa yi phyogs ni thams cad dang // sgo khyung gyi ni 'tshams rnams su// rdo rje rin chen spras
33b3(1): ba ni// dkyil 'khor phyi rim thig gdab bo// de yi rim pa'i nang zhugs la// 'khor lo 'dra bar rdo rje yi// thog gis yongs su bskor bar bya// ka ba brgyad kyis mdzes bgyis la/ 
33b4(1): ka ba'i nang logs su// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lngas brgyan la// dbus kyi dkyil 'khor dbus su ni// sangs rgyas kyi ni gzugs bzhag cing // sangs rgyas kyi ni phyogs kun gyi/ 
33b5(1): dkyil 'khor rnams kyi dbus rnams su// rim bzhin du ni dam rig mchog/ bzhi po legs par bzhag par gyi// dkyil 'khor bzhi po de dag tu// rdo rje'i gom pas song nas ni/ 
33b6(1): mi g.yo ba la sogs pa yi// sangs rgyas bzhi po thams cad bzhag/ mi g.yo ba yi dkyil 'khor du// rdo rje 'dzin sogs mnyam par bzhag/ rin chen 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor dus
33b7(1): rdo rje snying sogs rdzogs par bzhug/ tshe dpag med pa'i dkyil 'khor du// rdo rje spyan sogs dag par bzhag/ gdon mi za grub dkyil 'khor du// rdo rje rgya gram la sogs bzhag/ 'khor lo'i/ 
33b8(1): grwa yaM rnams su// rdo rje lha mo rnams kyang bzhag/ dkyil 'khor phyi rim grwa rnams su// sangs rgyas mchod pa rnams kyang bzhag/ sgo rnams kun gyi nang du ni// sgo srungs bzhi yang bzhag par
35a1(1): par bsdus par gyur pa/ bla na med pa'i dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / rangs pa rnams 'byung bar byed pa der ni/ bslab pa'i gzhis 'jigs shing skrag nas mi 'jug
35a2(1): ba dag kyang mchis te/ de dag ngan song gi dkyil 'khor gyi lam du 'jug par kha bltas shing gnas pa rnams kyang dga' ba dang mgu ba'i dam pa thams cad grub cing / bde ba dang yid bde ba
35a3(1): myong bar bgyi ba dang / ngan song gi rgyud thams cad du 'jug par kha bltas pa'i lam las zlog par bgyi ba'i slad du rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po 'dir 'jug tu rung ngo // bcom ldan
35a4(1): 'das chos can gyi sems can de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi tshul khrims dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / shes rab kyi dngos grub dam pa'i thabs kyis sangs rgyas rnams kyi byang chub tshol ba na/ 
35a5(1): bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa la sogs pa dang / sa rnams kyis 'bad cing nyon mongs par gyur pa dag kyang mchis te/ de dag kyang rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po 'dir zhugs ma
35a6(1): thag tu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du grub pa yang rnyed par dka' ba ma lags na/ dngos grub gzhan lta smos kyang ci 'tshal/ de nas dang po kho na re shig de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
35a7(1): la phyag bzhi bgyi'o// de ni 'di ltar lus thams cad kyi rdo rje'i thal mo brkyang te/ phyag 'tshal zhing sngags 'di skad du/ oM sar+b+ba ta thA ga ta pU dzo bas+thA na ya Ang ma naM nir ta yA mi/ sarbA ta
35a8(1): thA ga tA badz+ra sa twa a ti hiSh+Tha sa mAM/ zhes brjod do// de nas de bzhin du 'dug ste// rdo rje'i thal mo snying kar bzhag ste/ dpral bar phyag bya zhing sngags 'di skad du/ oM sar+b+ba da thA ga ta pU dza a
35b1(1): gi ka ya yA na/ ni dras ya ma/ sarbA sa nags badz+ra ra d+hA ma dzu rgyum/ zhes brjod do// de nas de bzhin du 'dus ste/ rdo rje la ma spu bong sbyar te/ khas phyag 'tshal zhing sngags da/ 
35b2(1): skad du/ oM sar+b+ba ta thA ga ta pU dza pra baR+Sha nA ya At+ma nAM/ nir+yA ta ya mAM/ sar+b+ba ta thA ga tA badz+ra d+har+m+ma pra baR+Sha ya mAM/ zhes brjod do// de nas de bzhin du 'dug ste/ rdo rje thal mo spyi bo nas pa ba ste/ 
35b3(1): snying kar bzhag nas spyi bos phyag 'tshal zhing sngags 'di skad du/ oM sarba ta thA ga tA pu dza kar+m+ma ni At+ma nA nid+ya ta yA mi/ sar+b+ba ta thA ga tA badz+ra kar+m+ma ku ru mAM/ zhes brjod do// de nas bstod
35b4(1): g.yogs dang dmar po dkris nas/ sems dpa' rdo rje ma'i phyag rgya bcings la snying po 'di brjod do// sa ma ya s+t+waM/ de nas gung mo gnyis kyis me tog 'phreng ba 'dzin du bcug la/ drang zhing
35b5(1): snying po 'di brjod do// sa ma ya hUM/ de nas bcug ma thag tu 'di skad du sgoms shig/ deng khyod de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs su zhugs kyis/ ngas khyod la ye shes gang gis de
35b6(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du 'grub pa yang 'thob na// dngos grub gzhan lta smos kyang ci dgos te/ de lta bu'i rdo rje ye shes bskyed par byas/ khyod kyis dkyil 'khor chen po ma mthong ba rnams
35b7(1): lam spa shig/ dam cig nyams par gyur ta re/ de nas rdo rje slob dpon gyis sems dpa'i rdo rje'i phyag rgya kha nang du bstan pa dang / phyir bstan pa bcings pa rdo rje slob ma'i spyi bor bzhag ste/ 'di
35b8(1): skad du brjod par bya'o// 'di ni khyod kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig yin gyis gal te 'ga' zhig la smras na klang ba 'gas par gyur ro// de nas dam tshig gi phyag rgya de nyid dang mna'i chu'i snying pos sngag
36a1(1): la slob ma de 'thung ngu gzhug go/ de la mna'i snying po 'di yin te/ rdo rje sems dpa' nyid ni deng // khyod kyi snying la yang dag zhugs// gal te tshul 'di smras na ni// 
36a2(1): de ma thag tu dral te gshegs// oM badz+rod ka Tha/ de nas slob ma la 'di skad sgos shig/ deng phyin chad khyod kyi phyag na rdo rje nga yin gyis/ nga yis 'di byos shig ces bsgo ba gang yin pa de bya dgos
